		}
	}
	
	"OnChannelInterrupted"
	{
		"RemoveModifier"
		{
			"Target"			"CASTER"

		}
		
		"RemoveModifier"
		{
			"Target"			"CASTER"
			"ModifierName"		"modifier_rearm_level_2_datadriven"
		}
		
		"RemoveModifier"
		{
			"Target"			"CASTER"
			"ModifierName"		"modifier_rearm_level_3_datadriven"
		}
	}
	
	"OnChannelSucceeded"
	{
		"RunScript"
		{
			"ScriptFile"		"heroes/hero_tinker/rearm.lua"
			"Function"			"rearm_refresh_cooldown"
		}
	}
